          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          margin: auto;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

        }

          overflow-y: auto;

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

. It seems like due to async permission request flow, the prompt is destroyed during chip destructor is executed. From the crash log it seems like the problem is in `GetWidget()` 



<span class="line"><!---->. It seems like due to async permission request flow, the prompt is destroyed during chip destructor is executed. From the crash log it seems like the problem is in `GetWidget()` <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/permission_request_chip.cc;l=130



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/permission_request_chip.cc;l=130"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ui/views/location_bar/permission_request_chip.cc;l=130<!----></a>

In the past we had 2 step destruction in `LocationBarView::FinalizeChip()`:



<span class="line"><!---->In the past we had 2 step destruction in `LocationBarView::FinalizeChip()`:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Unsubscribe a chip from `prompt_bubble_->GetWidget();`



<span class="line"><!---->1. Unsubscribe a chip from `prompt_bubble_-&gt;GetWidget();`<!----></span>



<br>

My read is that prompt_bubble_ is UAF here, prompt_bubble_ is set to nullptr in OnWidgetClosing but that doesn't happen if the OS destroys the widget I believe. Presumably OnWidgetDestroying or OnWidgetDestroyed would be a good place to catch this. (This API makes for some good foot shooting. Maybe we need to make sure that OnWidgetClosing is called even during OS Widget destruction.)



<span class="line"><!---->My read is that prompt_bubble_ is UAF here, prompt_bubble_ is set to nullptr in OnWidgetClosing but that doesn't happen if the OS destroys the widget I believe. Presumably OnWidgetDestroying or OnWidgetDestroyed would be a good place to catch this. (This API makes for some good foot shooting. Maybe we need to make sure that OnWidgetClosing is called even during OS Widget destruction.)<!----></span>

Date: Thu Aug 19 11:10:45 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Thu Aug 19 11:10:45 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.



<span class="line"><!---->Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget->Close()/CloseNow() is



<span class="line"><!---->OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget-&gt;Close()/CloseNow() is<!----></span>



<br>





called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that



<span class="line"><!---->called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that<!----></span>



<br>





PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is



<span class="line"><!---->PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is<!----></span>



<br>





executed, which may lead to  UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->executed, which may lead to  UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To prevent UAF:



<span class="line"><!---->To prevent UAF:<!----></span>



<br>





* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from



<span class="line"><!---->* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from<!----></span>



<br>





widget observer.



<span class="line"><!---->widget observer.<!----></span>



<br>





* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.



<span class="line"><!---->* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.<!----></span>



<br>

Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.



<span class="line"><!---->Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget->Close()/CloseNow() is



<span class="line"><!---->OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget-&gt;Close()/CloseNow() is<!----></span>



<br>





called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that



<span class="line"><!---->called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that<!----></span>



<br>





PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is



<span class="line"><!---->PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is<!----></span>



<br>





executed, which may lead to  UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->executed, which may lead to  UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To prevent UAF:



<span class="line"><!---->To prevent UAF:<!----></span>



<br>





* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from



<span class="line"><!---->* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from<!----></span>



<br>





widget observer.



<span class="line"><!---->widget observer.<!----></span>



<br>





* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.



<span class="line"><!---->* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Date: Fri Aug 27 15:55:17 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Fri Aug 27 15:55:17 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.



<span class="line"><!---->Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget->Close()/CloseNow() is



<span class="line"><!---->OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget-&gt;Close()/CloseNow() is<!----></span>



<br>





called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that



<span class="line"><!---->called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that<!----></span>



<br>





PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is



<span class="line"><!---->PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is<!----></span>



<br>





executed, which may lead to  UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->executed, which may lead to  UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To prevent UAF:



<span class="line"><!---->To prevent UAF:<!----></span>



<br>





* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from



<span class="line"><!---->* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from<!----></span>



<br>





widget observer.



<span class="line"><!---->widget observer.<!----></span>



<br>





* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.



<span class="line"><!---->* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>



<br>





Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.



<span class="line"><!---->Migrate PermissionChip to OnWidgetDestroying.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget->Close()/CloseNow() is



<span class="line"><!---->OnWidgetClosing is notified only after widget-&gt;Close()/CloseNow() is<!----></span>



<br>





called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that



<span class="line"><!---->called. In case of ~Window() is triggered, there is a chance that<!----></span>



<br>





PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is



<span class="line"><!---->PermissionPromptBubble will be deleted before chip cleanup logic is<!----></span>



<br>





executed, which may lead to  UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->executed, which may lead to  UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To prevent UAF:



<span class="line"><!---->To prevent UAF:<!----></span>



<br>





* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from



<span class="line"><!---->* PermissionChip implements OnWidgetDestroying to unsubscribe from<!----></span>



<br>





widget observer.



<span class="line"><!---->widget observer.<!----></span>



<br>





* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.



<span class="line"><!---->* ViewTracker is used to track a permission prompt bubble state.<!----></span>



<br>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
